      <!-- PRODUCTS CAROUSEL -->
      <script type="text/javascript">
       function Next_ClientClick()
       {
           var intNumOfItemPerRow = parseInt(document.getElementById('ContentPlaceHolderFull_ucProdCarousel_hdNumOfItemPerRow').value);
           var intTotal = parseInt(document.getElementById('ContentPlaceHolderFull_ucProdCarousel_hdTotalItemNum').value);
           var intCurItemIndex = document.getElementById('ContentPlaceHolderFull_ucProdCarousel_hdCurItemIndex').value == "" ? 0 : parseInt(document.getElementById('ContentPlaceHolderFull_ucProdCarousel_hdCurItemIndex').value);
           var intNextItemIndex = (intCurItemIndex == intTotal - intNumOfItemPerRow ? intCurItemIndex : intCurItemIndex + 1);
           CDisplayProducts(intNextItemIndex, intTotal);
       }
 
       function Prev_ClientClick()
       {
           var intTotal = parseInt(document.getElementById('ContentPlaceHolderFull_ucProdCarousel_hdTotalItemNum').value);
           var intCurItemIndex = document.getElementById('ContentPlaceHolderFull_ucProdCarousel_hdCurItemIndex').value == "" ? 0 : parseInt(document.getElementById('ContentPlaceHolderFull_ucProdCarousel_hdCurItemIndex').value);
           var intNextItemIndex = (intCurItemIndex == 0 ? intCurItemIndex : intCurItemIndex - 1);
           CDisplayProducts(intNextItemIndex, intTotal);
       }
       
       function CDisplayProducts(nextItemIndex, totalItemNum)
       {
           var numOfItemPerRow = parseInt(document.getElementById('ContentPlaceHolderFull_ucProdCarousel_hdNumOfItemPerRow').value);
 
           //For the repeater's ItemArray ( pnlProductItem ); the 2nd line has the same function, just in case the 1st doesn't work for some browser
           var productCarouselItemArray = document.getElementsByClassName("ProductCarouselItems");
           if (productCarouselItemArray == null) productCarouselItemArray = $(".ProductCarouselItems");   
           
           for (var i = 0; i < productCarouselItemArray.length; i++)
           {
               if (i < nextItemIndex || i >= nextItemIndex + numOfItemPerRow)
                   productCarouselItemArray[i].attributes["style"].value = "display:none";   //.Visible = false;
               else
                   productCarouselItemArray[i].attributes["style"].value = "display:block";  //.Visible = true;
           }
           
           //For btnNext, btnPrevious
           if (nextItemIndex >= totalItemNum - numOfItemPerRow)
               document.getElementById('ContentPlaceHolderFull_ucProdCarousel_lbtnNext').attributes["style"].value = "display:none";
           else
               document.getElementById('ContentPlaceHolderFull_ucProdCarousel_lbtnNext').attributes["style"].value = "display:block";
 
           if (nextItemIndex <= 0)
               document.getElementById('ContentPlaceHolderFull_ucProdCarousel_lbtnPrev').attributes["style"].value = "display:none"; 
           else
               document.getElementById('ContentPlaceHolderFull_ucProdCarousel_lbtnPrev').attributes["style"].value = "display:block";
             
           //Set the hdCurItemIndex
           document.getElementById('ContentPlaceHolderFull_ucProdCarousel_hdCurItemIndex').value = nextItemIndex;
       }
      </script>

     <script type="text/javascript">
      function ChangeCatalog() {
         var eCtrlID = '#changeCat1_eID_hf';
         var ouCtrlID = '#changeCat1_cOU_hf';
         var panelID = '#changeCat1_changeCat_panel';
         var callingPageCtrlID = '#changeCat1_callingPage_hf';
         var generalError = "<p>I'm sorry. There was an error processing your request. The web service could not be accessed or did not respond as expected. Please contact the site administrator.</p>";
         var div = $('#ChangeCatContentWrapper');
         var confirmChangeBtn = $('#changeCat1_confirmChange_link');
         var saveCatChangeBtn = $('#changeCat1_saveCatChange');
         var htmlStr = ''
         var autoUpd = new XMLHttpRequest;
         var urlService = "/WebServices/CommonWebService.asmx/GetRadioButtonOrgUnitList";
         var isError = false;
 
         if (confirmChangeBtn.hasClass('ui-helper-hidden') == false)
             confirmChangeBtn.addClass('ui-helper-hidden');
 
         if (saveCatChangeBtn.hasClass('ui-helper-hidden') == false)
             saveCatChangeBtn.addClass('ui-helper-hidden');
 
         if (!isError & document.location.toString().indexOf('ChangeOrgUnit') < 1) {
             autoUpd = $.ajax({
                 type: "POST",
                 url: urlService,
                 data: { employeeID: $(eCtrlID).val(), currentOrgUnitID: $(ouCtrlID).val(), callingPage: $(callingPageCtrlID).val() },
                 context: div
             })
             .done(function (jqxhr, textStatus, exc) {
                 var htmlStr = (jqxhr.text == null) ? (jqxhr.firstChild.textContent == null ? generalError : jqxhr.firstChild.textContent) : jqxhr.text;
                 div.html(htmlStr);
 
                 if (htmlStr != '' & htmlStr != generalError)
                     saveCatChangeBtn.removeClass('ui-helper-hidden');
 
                 ShowCCModalPopup();
             });
         } else {
             div.html(generalError);   
         }
 
         return false;
     }
 
     function UpdateSelectedCatalog(orgUnitID) {
         var div = $('#ChangeCatContentWrapper');
         var confirmChangeBtn = $('#changeCat1_confirmChange_link');
         var htmlStr = ''
         var autoUpd = new XMLHttpRequest;
         var urlService = "/WebServices/CommonWebService.asmx/ChangeCatalogUpdate";
         var isError = false;
 
         if (!isError) {
             autoUpd = $.ajax({
                 type: "POST",
                 url: urlService,
                 data: { selectedOrgUnitID: orgUnitID },
                 context: div
             })
             .done(function (jqxhr, textStatus, exc) {
                 var htmlStr = (jqxhr.text == null) ? jqxhr.firstChild.textContent : jqxhr.text;
                 div.html('<p>' + htmlStr + '</p>');
 
                 if (htmlStr.toLowerCase().indexOf("error-") >= 0) {
                     div.html('<p>' + htmlStr + '</p>');
                     ShowCCModalPopup();
                     confirmChangeBtn.addClass('ui-helper-hidden')
                 }
                 else {
                     HideCCModalPopup();
                     document.location.reload();
                 }
             }).fail(function () {
                 div.html('<p>The request failed to find the proper service. Please try again or contact the site administrator.</p>');
                 confirmChangeBtn.addClass('ui-helper-hidden')
             });
         } else {
             div.html('<p>I&#39;m sorry. There was an error processing your request. Please contact the site administrator.</p>');
             confirmChangeBtn.addClass('ui-helper-hidden')
         }
 
 
         return false;
     }
 
     function ConfirmCatalogChange() {
         var urlService = "/WebServices/CommonWebService.asmx/ConfirmCatalogChange";
         var newOrgUnitID = $('input[name="changeCatalogOrgList"][type="radio"]:checked').val();
         var confirmmessage = '';
         var confirmWebReq = new XMLHttpRequest;
         var div = $('#ChangeCatContentWrapper');
         var confirmChangeBtn = $('#changeCat1_confirmChange_link');
         var saveCatChangeBtn = $('#changeCat1_saveCatChange');
 
         saveCatChangeBtn.addClass('ui-helper-hidden');
 
         confirmWebReq = $.ajax({
             type: "POST",
             url: urlService,
             data: {},
             context: div
         })
         .done(function (jqxhr, textStatus, exc) {
             confirmmessage = (jqxhr.text == null) ? jqxhr.firstChild.textContent : jqxhr.text;
             confirmChangeBtn.removeClass('ui-helper-hidden');
             confirmChangeBtn.attr('onclick', 'return UpdateSelectedCatalog(' + newOrgUnitID + ')');
             div.html(confirmmessage);
         }).fail(function () {
             confirmmessage = '<p>The request failed to find the proper service. Please try again or contact the site administrator.</p>';
             confirmChangeBtn.addClass('ui-helper-hidden')
             div.html(confirmmessage);
         });
 
         return false;
     }
 
     function ShowCCModalPopup() {
         $find("CCModalBehavior").show();
     }
 
     function HideCCModalPopup() {
         $find("CCModalBehavior").hide();
     }
     </script>
